	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Hyperbola</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Plane curve: conic section</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This article is about a geometric curve. For the term used in rhetoric, see <a href="/wiki/Hyperbole" title="Hyperbole">Hyperbole</a>.</div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:212px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbola_(PSF).svg" class="image"><img alt="The image shows a double cone in which a geometrical plane has sliced off parts of the top and bottom half; the boundary curve of the slice on the cone is the hyperbola. A double cone consists of two cones stacked point-to-point and sharing the same axis of rotation; it may be generated by rotating a line about an axis that passes through a point of the line." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Hyperbola_%28PSF%29.svg/210px-Hyperbola_%28PSF%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="210" height="330" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Hyperbola_%28PSF%29.svg/315px-Hyperbola_%28PSF%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Hyperbola_%28PSF%29.svg/420px-Hyperbola_%28PSF%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="854" data-file-height="1341" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbola_(PSF).svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A hyperbola is an open curve with two branches, the intersection of a <a href="/wiki/Plane_(geometry)" title="Plane (geometry)">plane</a> with both halves of a double cone. The plane does not have to be parallel to the axis of the cone; the hyperbola will be symmetrical in any case.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-def-ass-e.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Hyperbel-def-ass-e.svg/300px-Hyperbel-def-ass-e.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="248" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Hyperbel-def-ass-e.svg/450px-Hyperbel-def-ass-e.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Hyperbel-def-ass-e.svg/600px-Hyperbel-def-ass-e.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="296" data-file-height="245" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-def-ass-e.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola (red): features</div></div></div>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Mathematics" title="Mathematics">mathematics</a>, a <b>hyperbola</b> (plural <i>hyperbolas</i> or <i>hyperbolae</i>) is a type of <a href="/wiki/Smooth_function" class="mw-redirect" title="Smooth function">smooth</a> <a href="/wiki/Plane_curve" title="Plane curve">curve lying in a plane</a>, defined by its geometric properties or by equations for which it is the solution set.  A hyperbola has two pieces, called <a href="/wiki/Connected_component_(graph_theory)" class="mw-redirect" title="Connected component (graph theory)">connected components</a> or branches, that are mirror images of each other and resemble two infinite <a href="/wiki/Bow_(weapon)" class="mw-redirect" title="Bow (weapon)">bows</a>.  The hyperbola is one of the three kinds of <a href="/wiki/Conic_section" title="Conic section">conic section</a>, formed by the intersection of a <a href="/wiki/Plane_(mathematics)" class="mw-redirect" title="Plane (mathematics)">plane</a> and a double <a href="/wiki/Cone_(geometry)" class="mw-redirect" title="Cone (geometry)">cone</a>.  (The other conic sections are the <a href="/wiki/Parabola" title="Parabola">parabola</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Ellipse" title="Ellipse">ellipse</a>. A <a href="/wiki/Circle" title="Circle">circle</a> is a special case of an ellipse.) If the plane intersects both halves of the double cone but does not pass through the apex of the cones, then the conic is a hyperbola.
</p><p>Hyperbolas arise in many ways: 
</p>
<ul><li>as the curve representing the function <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)=1/x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo>/</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)=1/x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/049b4bda6d9e222e496f2670248d9ecfb75841d1" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:11.171ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="f(x) = 1/x"/></span> in the <a href="/wiki/Cartesian_coordinate_system" title="Cartesian coordinate system">Cartesian plane</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>as the path followed by the shadow of the tip of a <a href="/wiki/Sundial" title="Sundial">sundial</a>,</li>
<li>as the shape of an <a href="/wiki/Open_orbit" class="mw-redirect" title="Open orbit">open orbit</a> (as distinct from a closed elliptical orbit), such as the orbit of a <a href="/wiki/Spacecraft" title="Spacecraft">spacecraft</a> during a <a href="/wiki/Gravity_assist" title="Gravity assist">gravity assisted</a> swing-by of a planet or more generally any spacecraft exceeding the <a href="/wiki/Escape_velocity" title="Escape velocity">escape velocity</a> of the nearest planet,</li>
<li>as the path of a single-apparition <a href="/wiki/Comet" title="Comet">comet</a> (one travelling too fast ever to return to the solar system),</li>
<li>as the <a href="/wiki/Rutherford_scattering" title="Rutherford scattering">scattering trajectory</a> of a <a href="/wiki/Subatomic_particle" title="Subatomic particle">subatomic particle</a> (acted on by repulsive instead of attractive forces but the principle is the same),</li>
<li>in <a href="/wiki/Hyperbolic_navigation" title="Hyperbolic navigation">radio navigation</a>, when the difference between distances to two points, but not the distances themselves, can be determined,</li></ul>
<p>and so on.
</p><p>Each <a href="/wiki/Branch_(mathematics)" class="mw-redirect" title="Branch (mathematics)">branch</a> of the hyperbola has two arms which become straighter (lower curvature) further out from the center of the hyperbola. Diagonally opposite arms, one from each branch, tend in the limit to a common line, called the <a href="/wiki/Asymptote" title="Asymptote">asymptote</a> of those two arms. So there are two asymptotes, whose intersection is at the center of <a href="/wiki/Symmetry" title="Symmetry">symmetry</a> of the hyperbola, which can be thought of as the mirror point about which each branch reflects to form the other branch. In the case of the curve <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)=1/x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>f</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo>/</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)=1/x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/049b4bda6d9e222e496f2670248d9ecfb75841d1" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:11.171ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="f(x) = 1/x"/></span> the asymptotes are the two <a href="/wiki/Coordinate_axes" class="mw-redirect" title="Coordinate axes">coordinate axes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hyperbolas share many of the ellipses' analytical properties such as <a href="/wiki/Eccentricity_(mathematics)" title="Eccentricity (mathematics)">eccentricity</a>, <a href="/wiki/Focus_(geometry)" title="Focus (geometry)">focus</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Directrix_(conic_section)" class="mw-redirect" title="Directrix (conic section)">directrix</a>. Typically the correspondence can be made with nothing more than a change of sign in some term. Many other <a href="/wiki/Mathematical_object" title="Mathematical object">mathematical objects</a> have their origin in the hyperbola, such as <a href="/wiki/Hyperbolic_paraboloid" class="mw-redirect" title="Hyperbolic paraboloid">hyperbolic paraboloids</a> (saddle surfaces), <a href="/wiki/Hyperboloid" title="Hyperboloid">hyperboloids</a> ("wastebaskets"), <a href="/wiki/Hyperbolic_geometry" title="Hyperbolic geometry">hyperbolic geometry</a> (<a href="/wiki/Nikolai_Lobachevsky" title="Nikolai Lobachevsky">Lobachevsky</a>'s celebrated <a href="/wiki/Non-Euclidean_geometry" title="Non-Euclidean geometry">non-Euclidean geometry</a>), <a href="/wiki/Hyperbolic_function" title="Hyperbolic function">hyperbolic functions</a> (sinh, cosh, tanh, etc.), and <a href="/wiki/Gyrovector_space" title="Gyrovector space">gyrovector spaces</a> (a geometry proposed for use in both <a href="/wiki/Theory_of_relativity" title="Theory of relativity">relativity</a> and <a href="/wiki/Quantum_mechanics" title="Quantum mechanics">quantum mechanics</a> which is not <a href="/wiki/Euclidean_geometry" title="Euclidean geometry">Euclidean</a>).
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_and_history">Etymology and history</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Etymology and history">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The word "hyperbola" derives from the <a href="/wiki/Greek_language" title="Greek language">Greek</a> <span lang="grc" title="Ancient Greek language text">ὑπερβολή</span>, meaning "over-thrown" or "excessive", from which the English term <a href="/wiki/Hyperbole" title="Hyperbole">hyperbole</a> also derives. Hyperbolae were discovered by <a href="/wiki/Menaechmus" title="Menaechmus">Menaechmus</a> in his investigations of the problem of <a href="/wiki/Doubling_the_cube" title="Doubling the cube">doubling the cube</a>, but were then called sections of obtuse cones.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> The term hyperbola is believed to have been coined by <a href="/wiki/Apollonius_of_Perga" title="Apollonius of Perga">Apollonius of Perga</a> (c. 262–c. 190 BC) in his definitive work on the <a href="/wiki/Conic_section" title="Conic section">conic sections</a>, the <i>Conics</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> 
The names of the other two general conic sections, the <a href="/wiki/Ellipse" title="Ellipse">ellipse</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Parabola" title="Parabola">parabola</a>, derive from the corresponding Greek words for "deficient" and "applied"; all three names are borrowed from earlier Pythagorean terminology which referred to a comparison of the side of rectangles of fixed area with a given line segment. The rectangle could be "applied" to the segment (meaning, have an equal length), be shorter than the segment or exceed the segment.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Definition_of_a_hyperbola_as_locus_of_points">Definition of a hyperbola as locus of points</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Definition of a hyperbola as locus of points">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-def-e.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Hyperbel-def-e.svg/220px-Hyperbel-def-e.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="201" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Hyperbel-def-e.svg/330px-Hyperbel-def-e.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Hyperbel-def-e.svg/440px-Hyperbel-def-e.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="296" data-file-height="270" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-def-e.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: definition by the distances of points to two fixed points (foci)</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-def-dc.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Hyperbel-def-dc.svg/220px-Hyperbel-def-dc.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="164" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Hyperbel-def-dc.svg/330px-Hyperbel-def-dc.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/Hyperbel-def-dc.svg/440px-Hyperbel-def-dc.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="297" data-file-height="221" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-def-dc.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: definition with circular directrix</div></div></div>
<p>A hyperbola can be defined geometrically as a set of points (<a href="/wiki/Locus_of_points" class="mw-redirect" title="Locus of points">locus of points</a>) in the Euclidean plane:

<p>The midpoint <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M}">

</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f82cade9898ced02fdd08712e5f0c0151758a0dd" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.442ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="M"/></span> of the line segment joining the foci is called the <i>center</i> of the hyperbola.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> The line through the foci is called the <i>major axis</i>. It contains the <i>vertices</i> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle V_{1},V_{2}}">

The distance <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle c}">

The quotient <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\tfrac {c}{a}}}">

This property should not be confused with the definition of a hyperbola with help of a directrix (line) below.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Hyperbola_in_Cartesian_coordinates">Hyperbola in Cartesian coordinates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Hyperbola in Cartesian coordinates">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Equation">Equation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Equation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>If Cartesian coordinates are introduced such that the origin is the center of the hyperbola and the <i>x</i>-axis is the major axis, then the hyperbola is called <i>east-west-opening</i> and 
</p>
<dl><dd>the <i>foci</i> are the points <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle F_{1}=(c,0),\ F_{2}=(-c,0)}">

<p>For an arbitrary point <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle (x,y)}">

<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {(x-c)^{2}+y^{2}}}}">

<p>Remove the square roots by suitable squarings and use the relation <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle b^{2}=c^{2}-a^{2}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msup>
          <mi>b</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>2</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <msup>
          <mi>c</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>2</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <msup>
          <mi>a</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>2</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b^{2}=c^{2}-a^{2}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a7085e6f3d3da8fe61991b4540a149eb49bc88aa" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:12.336ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle b^{2}=c^{2}-a^{2}}"/></span> to obtain the equation of the hyperbola:
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {x^{2}}{a^{2}}}-{\frac {y^{2}}{b^{2}}}=1\ .}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <msup>
              <mi>x</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>2</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msup>
            <msup>
              <mi>a</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>2</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msup>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <msup>
              <mi>y</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>2</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msup>
            <msup>
              <mi>b</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>2</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msup>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
        <mo>.</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {x^{2}}{a^{2}}}-{\frac {y^{2}}{b^{2}}}=1\ .}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c704cf0bdb9ca00934c759b2439b27b656c20cd8" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.171ex; width:14.6ex; height:6.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {x^{2}}{a^{2}}}-{\frac {y^{2}}{b^{2}}}=1\ .}"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>This equation is called the <i>canonical form</i> of a hyperbola, because any hyperbola, regardless of its orientation relative to the Cartesian axes and regardless of the location of its center, can be transformed to this form by a change of variables, giving a hyperbola that is <a href="/wiki/Congruence_(geometry)" title="Congruence (geometry)">congruent</a> to the original (see <a href="#Quadratic_equation">below</a>).
</p><p>The axes of <a href="/wiki/Symmetry_(geometry)" title="Symmetry (geometry)">symmetry</a> or <i>principal axes</i> are the <i>transverse axis</i> (containing the segment of length 2<i>a</i> with endpoints at the vertices) and the <i>conjugate axis</i> (containing the segment of length 2<i>b</i> perpendicular to the transverse axis and with midpoint at the hyperbola's center).<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> As opposed to an ellipse, a hyperbola has only two vertices: <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle (a,0),\;(-a,0)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>a</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mspace width="thickmathspace" />
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>a</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (a,0),\;(-a,0)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/64733db39f339c01dcdfe786c9fe635f75eced12" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:13.958ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle (a,0),\;(-a,0)}"/></span>. The two points <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle (0,b),\;(0,-b)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>b</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mspace width="thickmathspace" />
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>b</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (0,b),\;(0,-b)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9738f7abe8b767a49be0890fc878f9cd5d988ae4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:13.494ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle (0,b),\;(0,-b)}"/></span> on the conjugate axis are <i>not</i> on the hyperbola.
</p><p>It follows from the equation that the hyperbola is <i>symmetric</i> with respect to both of the coordinate axes and hence symmetric with respect to the origin.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Eccentricity">Eccentricity</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Eccentricity">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>For a hyperbola in the above canonical form, the <a href="/wiki/Eccentricity_(mathematics)" title="Eccentricity (mathematics)">eccentricity</a> is given by
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" alttext="{\textstyle e={\sqrt {1+{\frac {b^{2}}{a^{2}}}}}.}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="false" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>e</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <msqrt>
            <mn>1</mn>
            <mo>+</mo>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
              <mfrac>
                <msup>
                  <mi>b</mi>
                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                    <mn>2</mn>
                  </mrow>
                </msup>
                <msup>
                  <mi>a</mi>
                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                    <mn>2</mn>
                  </mrow>
                </msup>
              </mfrac>
            </mrow>
          </msqrt>
        </mrow>
        <mo>.</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\textstyle e={\sqrt {1+{\frac {b^{2}}{a^{2}}}}}.}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9c733a9ec6f8f22a51bf54eddb0a26b432ecede4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:13.693ex; height:6.176ex;" alt="{\textstyle e={\sqrt {1+{\frac {b^{2}}{a^{2}}}}}.}"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>Two hyperbolas are <a href="/wiki/Similarity_(geometry)" title="Similarity (geometry)">geometrically similar</a> to each other – meaning that they have the same shape, so that one can be transformed into the other by <a href="/wiki/Translation_(mathematics)" class="mw-redirect" title="Translation (mathematics)">rigid left and right movements</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rotation_(mathematics)" title="Rotation (mathematics)">rotation</a>, <a href="/wiki/Reflection_(mathematics)" title="Reflection (mathematics)">taking a mirror image</a>, and scaling (magnification) – if and only if they have the same eccentricity.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Asymptotes">Asymptotes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Asymptotes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-param-e.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Hyperbel-param-e.svg/250px-Hyperbel-param-e.svg.png" decoding="async" width="250" height="194" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Hyperbel-param-e.svg/375px-Hyperbel-param-e.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Hyperbel-param-e.svg/500px-Hyperbel-param-e.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="296" data-file-height="230" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-param-e.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: semi-axes <i>a</i>,<i>b</i>, linear eccentricity <i>c</i>, semi latus rectum <i>p</i></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbola-3prop.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Hyperbola-3prop.svg/300px-Hyperbola-3prop.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="198" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Hyperbola-3prop.svg/450px-Hyperbola-3prop.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Hyperbola-3prop.svg/600px-Hyperbola-3prop.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="297" data-file-height="196" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbola-3prop.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: 3 properties</div></div></div>
<p>Solving the equation (above) of the hyperbola for <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle y}">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle y=\pm {\frac {b}{a}}{\sqrt {x^{2}-a^{2}}}.}">

<p>It follows from this that the hyperbola approaches the two lines

<p>for large values of <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle |x|}">

These two lines intersect at the center (origin) and are called <i>asymptotes</i> of the hyperbola <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\tfrac {x^{2}}{a^{2}}}-{\tfrac {y^{2}}{b^{2}}}=1\ .}">

<p>From the <a href="/wiki/Hesse_normal_form" title="Hesse normal form">Hesse normal form</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\tfrac {bx\pm ay}{\sqrt {a^{2}+b^{2}}}}=0}">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\color {magenta}{(2)}}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

            </mrow>
          </mstyle>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\color {magenta}{(2)}}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/78f36ad867c1f999bbad253b86be45dd4a7369ad" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:2.972ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle {\color {magenta}{(2)}}}"/></span> The <i>product of the distances from a point on the hyperbola to both the asymptotes</i> is the constant <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\tfrac {a^{2}b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}}\ ,}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Semi-latus_rectum">Semi-latus rectum</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Semi-latus rectum">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The length of the chord through one of the foci, perpendicular to the major axis of the hyperbola, is called the <i>latus rectum</i>. One half of it is the <i>semi-latus rectum</i> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle p}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>p</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="p"/></span>. A calculation shows
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle p={\frac {b^{2}}{a}}.}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>p</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <msup>
              <mi>b</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>2</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msup>
            <mi>a</mi>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mo>.</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p={\frac {b^{2}}{a}}.}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4666011d678a26069261a7b5ee4951671d22e721" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:7.892ex; height:5.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle p={\frac {b^{2}}{a}}.}"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>The semi-latus rectum <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle p}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>p</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="p"/></span> may also be viewed as the <i><a href="/wiki/Radius_of_curvature" title="Radius of curvature">radius of curvature</a> </i> of the <a href="/wiki/Osculating_circle" title="Osculating circle">osculating circles</a> at the vertices.
</p>

                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mn>2</mn>
                </mrow>
              </msubsup>
              <msup>
                <mi>a</mi>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mn>2</mn>
                </mrow>
              </msup>
            </mfrac>
          </mstyle>
        </mrow>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mstyle displaystyle="false" scriptlevel="0">
            <mfrac>
              <msubsup>
                <mi>y</mi>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

              <msup>
                <mi>b</mi>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mn>2</mn>
                </mrow>
              </msup>
            </mfrac>
          </mstyle>
        </mrow>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\tfrac {x_{0}^{2}}{a^{2}}}-{\tfrac {y_{0}^{2}}{b^{2}}}=1}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/33b8848b7dfa7ee5c065050044a7f2b58351e402" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.671ex; width:12.198ex; height:5.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle {\tfrac {x_{0}^{2}}{a^{2}}}-{\tfrac {y_{0}^{2}}{b^{2}}}=1}"/></span>, the equation of the tangent at point <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle (x_{0},y_{0})}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>x</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>0</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <msub>

            <mn>0</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (x_{0},y_{0})}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/29c296094af9a1c665425debeac5eaab99a37a04" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:7.421ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="(x_{0},y_{0})"/></span> is
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {x_{0}}{a^{2}}}x-{\frac {y_{0}}{b^{2}}}y=1.}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <msub>
              <mi>x</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>0</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msub>

              <mi>a</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>2</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msup>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <msub>
              <mi>y</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>0</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msub>
            <msup>
              <mi>b</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>2</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msup>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mi>y</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>1.</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {x_{0}}{a^{2}}}x-{\frac {y_{0}}{b^{2}}}y=1.}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/51aed2a1a1d02f033c3ad34f6de5c0d641a863ee" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.171ex; width:16.483ex; height:5.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {x_{0}}{a^{2}}}x-{\frac {y_{0}}{b^{2}}}y=1.}"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>A particular tangent line distinguishes the hyperbola from the other conic sections.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Let <i>f</i> be the distance from the vertex <i>V</i> (on both the hyperbola and its axis through the two foci) to the nearer focus. Then the distance, along a line perpendicular to that axis, from that focus to a point P on the hyperbola is greater than 2<i>f</i>. The tangent to the hyperbola at P intersects that axis at point Q at an angle ∠PQV of greater than 45°.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rectangular_hyperbola">Rectangular hyperbola</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Rectangular hyperbola">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the case <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle a=b}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>a</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>b</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a=b}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1956b03d1314c7071ac1f45ed7b1e29422dcfcc4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.326ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="a=b"/></span> the hyperbola is called <i>rectangular</i> (or <i>equilateral</i>), because its asymptotes intersect rectangularly (that is, are perpendicular). For this case, the linear eccentricity is <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle c={\sqrt {2}}a}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>c</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <msqrt>
            <mn>2</mn>
          </msqrt>
        </mrow>
        <mi>a</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle c={\sqrt {2}}a}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a30e073f8d65c68121d6ecf4393ed3a3a0cf968f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:8.433ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle c={\sqrt {2}}a}"/></span>, the eccentricity <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle e={\sqrt {2}}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>e</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <msqrt>
            <mn>2</mn>
          </msqrt>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e={\sqrt {2}}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ae37adc9a631c89e1f35d3446bea2b101f4b15a1" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:7.28ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle e={\sqrt {2}}}"/></span> and the semi-latus rectum <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle p=a}">
  <semantics>

        <mi>a</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p=a}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/25febe0653c986d735afa81927ce946065456384" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:5.587ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle p=a}"/></span>.
</p>
<h3><span id="Parametric_representation_with_hyperbolic_sine.2Fcosine"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Parametric_representation_with_hyperbolic_sine/cosine">Parametric representation with hyperbolic sine/cosine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Parametric representation with hyperbolic sine/cosine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Using the <a href="/wiki/Hyperbolic_function" title="Hyperbolic function">hyperbolic sine and cosine functions</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \cosh ,\sinh }">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjugate_hyperbola">Conjugate hyperbola</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Conjugate hyperbola">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Exchange <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">

    </mrow>

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7cea9e4ab174f79d21d316c7f8b3c98c4d062935" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.171ex; width:16.477ex; height:6.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {x^{2}}{b^{2}}}-{\frac {y^{2}}{a^{2}}}=-1\ .}"/></span></dd></dl>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Hyperbolic_functions">Hyperbolic functions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Hyperbolic functions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:298px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbolic_functions-2.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Hyperbolic_functions-2.svg/296px-Hyperbolic_functions-2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="296" height="259" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Hyperbolic_functions-2.svg/444px-Hyperbolic_functions-2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Hyperbolic_functions-2.svg/592px-Hyperbolic_functions-2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="437" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbolic_functions-2.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A ray through the <a href="/wiki/Unit_hyperbola" title="Unit hyperbola">unit hyperbola</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x^{2}\ -\ y^{2}\ =\ 1}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

        <mn>1</mn>

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x^{2}\ -\ y^{2}\ =\ 1}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d3e685a58d3346d2b9550bdef7a3c46d6dd6c987" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:14.023ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle x^{2}\ -\ y^{2}\ =\ 1}"/></span> in the point <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle (\cosh \,a,\,\sinh \,a)}">

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ce456e0dfe2fc4c6140f27ba9e76c94535117b08" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:15.79ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle (\cosh \,a,\,\sinh \,a)}"/></span>, where <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle a}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>a</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="a"/></span> is twice the area between the ray, the hyperbola, and the <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="x"/></span>-axis. For points on the hyperbola below the <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="x"/></span>-axis, the area is considered negative.</div></div></div>
<p>Just as the <a href="/wiki/Trigonometric_function" class="mw-redirect" title="Trigonometric function">trigonometric functions</a> are defined in terms of the unit circle, so also the <a href="/wiki/Hyperbolic_function" title="Hyperbolic function">hyperbolic functions</a> are defined in terms of the <a href="/wiki/Unit_hyperbola" title="Unit hyperbola">unit hyperbola</a>, as shown in this diagram.
</p><p>Let <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle a}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>a</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="a"/></span> be twice the area between the <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="x"/></span> axis and a ray through the origin intersecting the unit hyperbola and define <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle b=\cosh a}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>b</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>cosh</mi>
        <mo>&#x2061;<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
        <mi>a</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b=\cosh a}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1609e4748d35be6b3f64a1af6caf851ee1a22255" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:10.117ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle b=\cosh a}"/></span> as the horizontal coordinate of the intersection point.
Then, by the <a href="/wiki/Pythagorean_theorem" title="Pythagorean theorem">Pythagorean theorem</a>,

<p>Solving for <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle b}">

<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x=b=\cosh a={\frac {e^{a}+e^{-a}}{2}}.}">

<p>By defining <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle y}">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \sinh a={\sqrt {\cosh ^{2}a-1}}.}">

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sinh a={\sqrt {\cosh ^{2}a-1}}.}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a8d916057de4c26a3ceb2d18e21d7c0389e809fb" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:22.912ex; height:3.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \sinh a={\sqrt {\cosh ^{2}a-1}}.}"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>This implies the exponential form of the hyperbolic sine (<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle h}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>h</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle h}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b26be3e694314bc90c3215047e4a2010c6ee184a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.339ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="h"/></span> is the vertical coordinate of the intersection point):
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle y=h=\sinh a={\frac {e^{a}-e^{-a}}{2}}.}">

                </mrow>
              </msup>
            </mrow>
            <mn>2</mn>
          </mfrac>
        </mrow>
        <mo>.</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y=h=\sinh a={\frac {e^{a}-e^{-a}}{2}}.}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/06a0b88fe81f6c665b76b0bec1360013200aa33f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:27.528ex; height:5.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle y=h=\sinh a={\frac {e^{a}-e^{-a}}{2}}.}"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>Other hyperbolic functions are defined according to the hyperbolic cosine and hyperbolic sine, so for example
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \operatorname {tanh} a={\frac {\sinh a}{\cosh a}}={\frac {e^{2a}-1}{e^{2a}+1}}.}">

<p>Solving for <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle a}">

<h2><span id="Hyperbola_with_equation_y_.3D_A.2Fx"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hyperbola_with_equation_y_=_A/x">Hyperbola with equation <i>y</i> = <i>A</i>/<i>x</i></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Hyperbola with equation y = A/x">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-gs-hl.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Hyperbel-gs-hl.svg/220px-Hyperbel-gs-hl.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="225" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Hyperbel-gs-hl.svg/330px-Hyperbel-gs-hl.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Hyperbel-gs-hl.svg/440px-Hyperbel-gs-hl.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="224" data-file-height="229" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-gs-hl.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Rotating the coordinate system in order to describe a rectangular hyperbola as graph of a function</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbeln-gs-3.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Hyperbeln-gs-3.svg/220px-Hyperbeln-gs-3.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="221" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Hyperbeln-gs-3.svg/330px-Hyperbeln-gs-3.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Hyperbeln-gs-3.svg/440px-Hyperbeln-gs-3.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="261" data-file-height="262" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbeln-gs-3.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Three rectangular hyperbolas <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle y=A/x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<p>If the <i>xy</i>-coordinate system is <a href="/wiki/Rotation_matrix" title="Rotation matrix">rotated</a> about the origin by the angle <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle -45^{\circ }}">
  <semantics>

          <mn>45</mn>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mo>&#x2218;<!-- ∘ --></mo>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle -45^{\circ }}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1b599e135133e742e7d720f87f30feb1a8336fcb" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:5.187ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle -45^{\circ }}"/></span>  and new coordinates <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \xi ,\eta }">
  <semantics>

The rectangular hyperbola <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\tfrac {x^{2}-y^{2}}{a^{2}}}=1}">

Solving for <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \eta }">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Definition_of_a_hyperbola_by_the_directrix_property">Definition of a hyperbola by the directrix property</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Definition of a hyperbola by the directrix property">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-ll-e.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Hyperbel-ll-e.svg/300px-Hyperbel-ll-e.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="260" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Hyperbel-ll-e.svg/450px-Hyperbel-ll-e.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Hyperbel-ll-e.svg/600px-Hyperbel-ll-e.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="296" data-file-height="257" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-ll-e.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: directrix property</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-ll-def.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Hyperbel-ll-def.svg/300px-Hyperbel-ll-def.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="253" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Hyperbel-ll-def.svg/450px-Hyperbel-ll-def.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Hyperbel-ll-def.svg/600px-Hyperbel-ll-def.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="296" data-file-height="250" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-ll-def.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: definition with directrix property</div></div></div>
<p>The two lines at distance <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" alttext="{\textstyle d={\frac {a^{2}}{c}}}">

</p><p>For an arbitrary point <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle P}">

          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>2</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mfrac>
            <msup>
              <mi>c</mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>2</mn>
              </mrow>
            </msup>

              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

          </mrow>
        </msup>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mtext>&#xA0;</mtext>
        <mo>.</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle |PF_{1}|^{2}-{\frac {c^{2}}{a^{2}}}|Pl_{1}|^{2}=0\ .}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/710186e6b250fc1d9a3ca0e1a57235ab486f2617" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.171ex; width:23.932ex; height:6.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle |PF_{1}|^{2}-{\frac {c^{2}}{a^{2}}}|Pl_{1}|^{2}=0\ .}"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>The second case is proven analogously.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kegelschnitt-schar-ev.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Kegelschnitt-schar-ev.svg/220px-Kegelschnitt-schar-ev.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="254" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Kegelschnitt-schar-ev.svg/330px-Kegelschnitt-schar-ev.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Kegelschnitt-schar-ev.svg/440px-Kegelschnitt-schar-ev.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="261" data-file-height="301" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kegelschnitt-schar-ev.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Pencil of conics with a common vertex and common semi latus rectum</div></div></div>
<p>The <i>inverse statement</i> is also true and can be used to define a hyperbola (in a manner similar to the definition of a parabola):
</p><p>For any point <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle F}">

<p>(The choice <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle e=1}">

<dl><dt>Proof</dt>

The directrix <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle l}">

the major/minor semi axis <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle a,b}">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Hyperbola_as_plane_section_of_a_cone">Hyperbola as plane section of a cone</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Hyperbola as plane section of a cone">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:452px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-dandel-s.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Hyperbel-dandel-s.svg/450px-Hyperbel-dandel-s.svg.png" decoding="async" width="450" height="230" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Hyperbel-dandel-s.svg/675px-Hyperbel-dandel-s.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Hyperbel-dandel-s.svg/900px-Hyperbel-dandel-s.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="537" data-file-height="275" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-dandel-s.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola (red): two views of a cone and two Dandelin spheres <i>d</i><sub>1</sub>, <i>d</i><sub>2</sub></div></div></div>
<p>The intersection of an upright double cone by a plane not through the vertex with slope greater than the slope of the lines on the cone is a hyperbola (see diagram: red curve). In order to prove the defining property of a hyperbola (see above) one uses two <a href="/wiki/Dandelin_spheres" title="Dandelin spheres">Dandelin spheres</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle d_{1},d_{2}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msub>
          <mi>d</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>1</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>d</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>2</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle d_{1},d_{2}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/83b2d0fcdb302558f5c12c37fc4e8cd104113539" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:5.56ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="d_{1},d_{2}"/></span>, which are spheres that touch the cone along circles <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle c_{1}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

            <mn>1</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle c_{1}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/77b7dc6d279091d354e0b90889b463bfa7eb7247" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.061ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="c_{1}"/></span> , <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle c_{2}}">
  <semantics>

It turns out: <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle F_{1},F_{2}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

            <mn>1</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>F</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>2</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle F_{1},F_{2}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ddbaefad7d000285a069031a623cdc454e4b79e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:6.132ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="F_{1},F_{2}"/></span> are the <i>foci</i> of the hyperbola.
</p>
<ol><li>Let  <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle P}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>P</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle P}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b4dc73bf40314945ff376bd363916a738548d40a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.745ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="P"/></span> be an arbitrary point of the intersection curve .</li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Pin_and_string_construction">Pin and string construction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Pin and string construction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbola-pin-string.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/Hyperbola-pin-string.svg/300px-Hyperbola-pin-string.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="253" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/Hyperbola-pin-string.svg/450px-Hyperbola-pin-string.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6a/Hyperbola-pin-string.svg/600px-Hyperbola-pin-string.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="333" data-file-height="281" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbola-pin-string.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: Pin and string construction</div></div></div>
<p>The definition of a hyperbola by its foci and its circular directrices (see above) can be used for drawing an arc of it with help of pins, a string and a ruler <sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>:

Point <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle B}">

(2) A <i>string</i> with length <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle |AB|}">

(3) One end of the string is pinned at point <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle A}">

(4) Take a <i>pen</i> and hold the string tight to the edge of the ruler. <br />
(5) <i>Rotating</i> the ruler around <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle F_{2}}">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="The_tangent_bisects_the_angle_between_the_lines_to_the_foci">The tangent bisects the angle between the lines to the foci</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: The tangent bisects the angle between the lines to the foci">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-wh-s.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Hyperbel-wh-s.svg/300px-Hyperbel-wh-s.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="230" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Hyperbel-wh-s.svg/450px-Hyperbel-wh-s.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Hyperbel-wh-s.svg/600px-Hyperbel-wh-s.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="360" data-file-height="276" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-wh-s.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: the tangent bisects the lines through the foci</div></div></div>
<p>The tangent at a point <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle P}">

Line <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle w}">

In order to prove that <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle w}">

Hence <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle w}">

  </semantics>

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle P}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b4dc73bf40314945ff376bd363916a738548d40a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.745ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="P"/></span>. <br />
From the diagram and the <a href="/wiki/Triangle_inequality" title="Triangle inequality">triangle inequality</a> one recognizes that <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle |QF_{2}|&lt;|LF_{2}|+|QL|=2a+|QF_{1}|}">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Midpoints_of_parallel_chords">Midpoints of parallel chords</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hyperbola&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Midpoints of parallel chords">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-psehnen-s.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Hyperbel-psehnen-s.svg/220px-Hyperbel-psehnen-s.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="198" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Hyperbel-psehnen-s.svg/330px-Hyperbel-psehnen-s.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Hyperbel-psehnen-s.svg/440px-Hyperbel-psehnen-s.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="288" data-file-height="259" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-psehnen-s.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: the midpoints of parallel chords lie on a line.</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-sa-s.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Hyperbel-sa-s.svg/220px-Hyperbel-sa-s.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="224" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Hyperbel-sa-s.svg/330px-Hyperbel-sa-s.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Hyperbel-sa-s.svg/440px-Hyperbel-sa-s.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="251" data-file-height="256" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hyperbel-sa-s.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hyperbola: the midpoint of a chord is the midpoint of the corresponding chord of the asymptotes.</div></div></div>
<p>The midpoints of parallel chords of a hyperbola lie on a line through the center (see diagram).
</p><p>The points of any chord may lie on different branches of the hyperbola.
</p><p>The proof of the property on midpoints is best done for the hyperbola <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle y=1/x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>y</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo>/</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y=1/x}</annotation>
  </semantics>

Because any hyperbola is an affine image of the hyperbola <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle y=1/x}">

For two points <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle P=\left(x_{1},{\tfrac {1}{x_{1}}}\right),\ Q=\left(x_{2},{\tfrac {1}{x_{2}}}\right)}">
